proteſta proteſtacion reader gud reader ȝour leſt weill auiſit werk ȝe repreif conſider werly rede ofter anys weil ane blenk ſle poetry tanc ȝit forſoith ſet beſy pane couth mak brade plane kepand ſodroun bot oure awin langage ſpeke lerned quhen wes ane page na ȝit ſo clene ſudroun refuſe bot ſum worde pronuce nychboure doi like latine bene grewe termes ſum behuffit quhilum dum sum baſtard latyne frenſche ynglis ois quhare ſcant wes ſcottis nane vthir chois oure • oung ſelu • ſkant bot fouth langage want quhare cullour propirte keip ſentence thareto conſtrenit mak ſayng ſchort ſum tyme mare compendius likly ryme tharfor gude freyndis ane gympe ane bourd pray ȝou note euery worde worthye clerk hecht laurence vaile amang latyne ane grete clerk ſans faile grantis quhen twelf ȝeris bene diligent ſtudy virgil ſcant knew quhat ment thou freynde quhen beſt wene haue virgil red vndirſtand ſene richt ſentence perchance fer ſeik werk tuelfȝeris firſt making eik corecke quhen poete deceis thus ſmall faltis wiſe freynde hald thy pece adherand proteſtacioun thoch wylliame caxtoun compatioun virgill buk 〈…〉 preyt prois clepand virgill eneados quhilk ſayis frenſche tranſlait na thing ado therwith god wate na mare like deuil ſanct auſtin haue na thank tharfore bot lois pyne ſchamefully ſtorie peruerte reid werk harmes hert ſic ane buk ſentence ingyne suld intitulit▪ eftir poete diuine ornate goldin verſis mare gylt ſpitte diſſpite ſe thame ſpylt ſic ane wicht quhilk treuly myne entent knew neuir thre wordis quhat virgill ment fer chowpis conſtrenyt flyte thre firſt bukis ouerhippit quyte saiffing ane litill twiching polidorus tempeſt ſet furth eolus full ſimpilly owin gyſe virgill thame wrate al ane vther wyſe caxtoun puttis buke tone ſtorme furth ſent eolus neptone bot quha ſa redis virgill ſoithfaſtly sall fynd neptone ſayffit eneas nauy liſt ſchaw quhow ſtorie dido caxtoun hale peruertit ſo beſyde quhare fenis follow bochace rynnys ſo fer fra virgill mony place ſa prolixt tedious faſſyoun ferd buke eneadoun twiching luf dede dido quene tua part hys volume doth contene text virgill traiſtis tuelf part ſkars contenis ȝe may ſe fyft buke feiſtis funerall luſty gammys playis paleſtrall ouer hippit quite left behind na thynge therof ȝe ſall caxtoun fynd ſext buke eik grantis wantis hale therof vnderſtude taile callis fenȝete nocht beleif sa virgill perchance leif iuno venus goddis neuer mercury mar neptune iupiter fortun eik hir neceſſite sic thingis attentik ar wate ȝit admittis quent philoſophye haldis ſaulis hoppis fra body body mony thingis quhilk virgil rehers thocht write furth followand vers caxtouns ſchrinkes ſic lyke thing tel war fabil bot paſſage hell bot traiſtis welevnder derk poetrye hid great▪ wiſdome lernīg quha ilk ſext buk knewe virgil tharin ane hie phyloſophoure ſchew vnder cloudis dirk poetry hyd lyis thare mony notabill hiſtorie ſo poetis thare craftye curys ſimilitudis vthir quent figuris ſoithfaſt mater hide conſtrene fals traiſt weil cace thay fene thare art ſo make thare werkis fare ende virgill ſall declare eik al poſſibill eneas herculus theſeus hell pa quhilk na gabbing ſu • hly na lye ihone bochas genologie goddis declaris like ye may reid recollis troye quha liſt take hede quha wate gif viſioun thidder went arte magik sorcery enchantment faderis ſaul ſpeik mete liknes ſum vther ſpreit like ſprete samuell ge raſit kinge saul phitones wyll ſay virgill bene al trewe bot ſic thinges ar poſſibill ſchewe al dayis war illuſiouns deuillis werkis coniuratiouns thare bene ſa clerkis determe bliſſit god faith mare ferme inewch therof ſayne bot vnto caxtoun thus returne agane name cieteis pepyll bene ſo bad put caxtoun bot bene mad flude touer tyber write men may knaw thare forueyit quyte palent ciete euander king virgill planely makis reherſing stude quhare rome ſtandis cheif palice ſamyn buke eik mare heit malice one ſelf ryuer touir ſays planelye eneas ciete edifie thus aye tiber touer puttis quhilk mony hundreth mylis ſundry ſikkirly le wyſe authoris leyne eneas ſaw neuer touer ene touer diuidis grece vngary • tiber cheif flude italye touer kend ane grane riuer latyne hecht danubium 〈◊〉 gif tanayis clippis ſa flude diuidis ewrope fra aſia elikewiſe eik caxtoun vane criſpina clippis sibilla cwmane text virgil traiſtis v hate deyphebe douthter glantus quhilk eneas conuoyar hell quhat ſuld langer errouris duell thay bene ſo plane eik ſa mony fold hundreth part therof leif vnfold laſt ſext buke virgil al feris quhilk contenis ſtrang battellis weris ilk caxtoun ſo blaitlye lattis ouer ſlip hald toung ſchame bitand lip grete affers athir oiſt arraye armour eneas freſche gaye quent curious caſtis poeticall perfyte ſimilitudis examplis quharin virgil beris palme lawde caxtoun dreid thay ſuld lippi ſkaude durſt neuer twiche vark laike knalage becaus onderſtude virgil langage buk na mare like virgil dar lay nyght oule reſemblis papingay quharfor ȝou gentill redarisexhortacion reader beſeiche traiſt na wiſe werk ſiche quhilk beſt wit mycht atteyne virgillis verſis follow na thing feyne ȝe worthie nobillis redis werk thy caſt vther buke ſyde fer quhilk vnder cullour ſum ſtrange wycht frenſihly leyes vneth tuo wordis gais rycht nold ȝe traiſt ſaid thys dyſpite lyſt wyth man bukis flyite wyth na bogill browny debaite nowthir auld gaiſtis ſpretis dede lai • na man lakkin dyſpyſe werkis till authoris ſic wiſe twiching virgyllis honoure reuerence quho euer contrary mon ſtand defence bot buke foundin worth ſic thre quhen red warp ſeye thraw fire rent euery crum twiching parte 〈◊〉 vnto vnlerned people whoſe rudnes cannot onderſtand vyrgil lo ſum syne defende forbiddis euery wicht ſpell ther pater noſter richt correct ȝit mend vyrgill tranſlater blame vulgare ſtyle knaw quhat pane follow fute hate albeit thou think ſaying intricat traiſt weil folow ane fix ſentence mater rare practike difficul fer ſtrater thocht thyne ingyne eleuate hie wryte wayis liberte gif bene ane boundis conſtrenit bad wit perchance thocht haue fenis ryme ane ragmen twiſe al curiouſe bot tuentye part ſa ſentencius quha attaychit vnto ane ſtaik ſe may go forther wreil tre rycht ſo virgyllis text ibound may fle le fault found thocht wold tranſcend go beſyde werk remanis ſchame hide thus conſtrenit al nere may hald verſe go nane vthir way le ſum hiſtorie ſubtell worde ryme cauſis mak degreſſioun ſum tyme thocht tranſlatioun eloquence ſkant na luſty caſt oratry virgill wantis ſtudious brane comprehend ſentence lete neuer taiſt flude eloquence thus forſoith becauſe fre werke mare obſure gros perde quharof god wate virgil wyte thocht myne blunt text maiſt perfite ȝit perſaue weilevyrgilys workis meit wiſe lerned men comon people conſate king poetis ganis rurall eſtate freſche memor bowbardes ſcho quha takis go quhare haue ado ſonnys licht nauer wers traiſt thochte bak bricht beames doith fle grene gentill engynis breiſtis curagious sic ar che pepill ganys beſt v werk deſiris na lewit rebaldale full nobilite thys ſtorie alhale euery vertew belanging nobyll man ornate poete bettir ony pantand diſtriuis perſoun eneas ſay ſic ane eneas ȝit perfitly blaſonis grauite ȝi • ſkant weil exponit quhay trowis lat thaym interpret animal homo mony hundreth termes mo quhilk langage ſoithly iwene men tell cleirly quhat thay mene betuix genus ſexus ſpeties diuerſite leid ſeik iceiſſe obiectum ſubiectum alſua expert couth fynd termes tua quhilks ar al ryff amang clerkis ſculis euer foulis plungit lake pulis logitianis knawis myne entent vnderquhais boundis lurkis mony ſtrange went quhairfor proces mon lat bot ȝit twiching tongis penurite mene vnto compare fare latyne knawin maiſt perfite langage fyne mycht alſo percais cum lidder ſpede arbor lignum till lede fynde different propir termes twane tharto put circulotucioun nane rycht ſo ſpeich often tymes ſemblabill wordis compyle rymes god wate virgill ar termes many hunder till expone maid ane felloun blunder followe ala • erlye virgilis wordes weyne thare ſuld vnderſtand quhat meyne bewte ornate eloquence may al tyme kepit wyth ſentence sanct gregoure al forbiddis v tranſlate word eftir word ſentence folow algate quha halis quod wordes properteis ful oft verite ſentence ſleis ſamyn properteis may apply horatius art poetry preis ſais thou traiſt interprete worde efter word tranſlate mater lo repreuis haldis myſſemyng ay worde worde reduce ony thing ſay chaucere offence bot till excus lewit inſuffitience ſtandis beneth virgill gre vnder al grant ſelf le ſum caſe quha kend maiſter chaucere gretelie virgil offendit thocht bald repreif fer balder cirtes leif saying followit virgillis lantern forne eneas dido forſworn forſworne eneas fals admittis callis tratour al thus wenyng allone enee haue repreuit greitlie prynce poetes greiut ſaid virgil diligence ſpot cryme reproche ony offence eneas loif magnifye gif grantis maneſworne foulely cure crafty ingyne gais quyte tuelf ȝeris laubouris war worth ane myte cirtis virgil ſchawisgods wyl commaūdemēt ſhuld euer prefered haue firſt place men action doynges enee thyng dido cartage departing quhilkis goddis commandit made forne gif thare command made manſworne wair repreif thare diuinite na reproche vnto ſaid enee al feiſt quhare ilioneus spekis quene dido ſais thus thare cours fate ſet italie thus mycht ſcho pretend na iuſt cauſe quhi thoucht troianis eftir departis cartage sen thay declarit hir thare vayage reid ferde buke quhare quene dido wraith thare ſal ȝe fynd enee maid neuer aith promit band wicht hir abide thus manſworne may neuer betyde nane vnkindnes ſchaw depart bidding ioue reuthful hart sen command god obey ſuld vnder charge na wrangus deid may fall bot ſikkerlie reſſoun behuffis excuſe chaucere fra maner repruuis louing ladyis lilly quhite ſet virgil eneas wyte euer god wate womannis freynd ſay na mare gentil redaris heynd lat faltis offence pa thow prince af poetis mercy cry meneinuocaciō god thou king kinges lord eterne thow muſe gidare laid ſterne remitting treſpas euery mys throu chriſt thy ſonethe werk beginnes god neuer haue proſperyus ſucces bring v hewynly blys afald godhede ay leſting diſcrepance perſonis thre equale ane ſubſtance cal humyl hart milde caliope payne goddis wilde may thing bot harine wene chriſt treſt borne virgine quene thou saluiour mankind mye muſe neuer ȝit na ſinful liſt refuſe quhilk beſocht deuotelie ſupple albeit lang thy hie maieſte accordis ȝit condiſcend write thy excelland mercy loue perfite thou holy g • ſt confort ſanctifye ſpret ende wark thy glory bot forthirmare laware till diſcend forgif virgill gif offend pardoun thy ſcolar ſuffer ryme sen thou ane mortall man ſum tyme cais fail haue diſoenȝe thocht lew • leile hart eneados ¶the poete firſt proponyng entent declaris iunois wrath matalent battellis manthe propoſition hole work • diſcriue fra troyis boundis firſt fugitiue fate italie come coiſt lauyne ouer land ſe cachit meikill pyne force goddis aboue fra euery ſtede cruel iuno throw auld remembrit feid grete payne batelles ſufferit alſo goddis brocht latio belt ciete fra quham nobil fame latyne peopill taken thare name eik faderis princis alba comeinuocatione walleris grete rome alſua thow muſe declare cauſis quhy quhat maieſty offendit ſchaw quham ȝit quharefor goddis drery quene feil dangeris ſic trawell maid ſuſtene ane worthy man fulfillit pietie thare ſic greif heuinlie myndes one hie thare ane ancient cietenarratiōe •• hewinge cauſes wherfore iuno henderid troians hecht cartage quham hynis tire held heritage inemye till italie ſtanding fare plane mouth lang tyber ouer forgane mychty nobillis fule ſcules ſere maiſt expert crafty fait quhilk ane land iuno ſaid hir ſpeciall aboue otheris maid hir natiue land poſtponis ſche callit ſamo cartage ſet hir ſe thar war hir armes ſtude eik hir chare goddes ettillit gif werdes war contrare realme ſuperior maiſtres ladis bot cirtes netheles fatale ſiſters reuolf ſchaw ſche kend troiane blude ane pepill ſchuld diſcend valȝeand ware regne wyde quhare ſyne cartage ſuld bring vnto fynale rewyne clene diſtroye realme libia dredand iuno ferthirmare alſwa remembrand mortall anciant grekis hir leif dere troye lang tyme ſche led day ȝet cauſe wraith away cruell harme forȝet ne mynd full depe ygrauen hir breiſt vnkynd iugement paris preferrit venus diſpriſing hir bewte al troiane blude hir odious iupiter engenerit dardanus fra quham troianis come adultre ganymede reuyſt abo • e ſky made hym butler quhilk douchters offyce iuno hate fyre kindillit bricht hir gay cleithing lowis licht gan glete ſperkilland birn vp ane bleis hir ryal tretſis inflambit euil eis hir crownell picht wich mony precius ſtane infirit birnand flawis alhale natiue goddis wele ȝe duellinge place quhare ſall leynd remane cuntre heynd certis new remember fader anchiſes sic ſecrete takynnyis fatis wiſe schew reherſit ſayand thus son quhen ſic hunger thou ſtad ſal thou art caryit til ane ſtrange coiſt meiſſis conſumit ar loiſt thou art conſtrenyt thy burdis gnaw fret thou irkit may beleif get ane ſober dwellyng ſtede perpetually remember place nere faſt found firſt cietie thy hand dicht fowſeis wally hie ſtandand hunger taryit v ſa lang ſal makend miſcheuis ſtrang quharfor morow airlie ȝou pray firſt ſon vpriſis gladlie may serche inquire made det quhen thou optenit victorie thou ſal wirſchip god tybris wattry hewit haw quhilk thou ſeis mony iawp iaw bettis thir brayis ſchawing bankis doun ful flude flowing fra toun toun throw fertil feildis ſchering thare vnder liſt maiſt gentyl reuere habitacioun huge grete mychty cieteis cheif ſouerane ſette beand ſayd ilk god flude vnder depe douk doun quhare ſtude ſocht vnto wattir ground anone dernlye hid none wiſt quhare gone • ew wyth gryſis tyberinus ſad • eneas fand ſacrifice made nycht • led ſlepe left enee fute ſtertes anon gan ſe furth orient brycht mornyng ſonnis heuenlie beames newly ſpryng holl luffis handis quhare ſtude dewly wattir hint fra flude syne heuin wiſe hiseneas 〈◊〉 prayeris made nymphis al fludis blytht glade ȝe holy nymphis laurentum land quham fra freſche riueris euery ſtrand flowis rynnyng ſay clere thare begynnyng furth ſowrſſus ſere thou haly fader tyberyne tybris eik thy bliſſit flude diuine reſſaue eneas ȝou vnbekend laſt perillis defend gif thou takis grete ſkaithis au ow promittis aithis quhare euer thy louch fountane may found quhare euer ſo thi ſpring quhat ground flude maiſt pleſand ſal ouer alquhare hallow honorabill offerandis euermare hornit riuere ringand lord kyng ouer al fludis italie ryng help laſt requyre efter ſa fell perrellis dangeris ſere conforme thy promys orakill hy quhen ſayd furth nauy tua galeyis cheis ilk tyde doubill raw airis athir ſyde rollyng wele graithit thame syne inſtrukkit menȝe bot lo haiſt ene ſaw ane meruellus wounders thing knaw ane mylk quhite ſow within woddis lay apoun grene watteris bank way littir new ferryit ſtede ane cullour gryſis thretty hede qham deuote eneas gyſe vnto greteſt iuno ſacrifyce britnis hir flok followaris ſet offerit vp altaris tyber hir ſwelland fludis mycht lang euer quhil dayis lycht stabillis calmis awin wyl ſtreme bakwa • ti vpflowis ſoft ſtill ſic wiſe meſand wattir ane ſtandand ſtank ſemyd ſmoth pule dub loun fare thy airis mycht findin na contrare therfor eneas tyme eſpy haiſtis wayage beſely wyth proſper cours ſobir quhiſpering pikkit bargis fir faſt thring ſlidis throw ſchaldis ſtil clere watter ferlies thare farde bere foreſt accuſtumate ſe sic thyngis wounderis quhat thys ſuld behald ſchynand ſcheildis fer mennys ſthulderis ay cummand nere nere payntit caruillis fleting throw flud bayth nycht day ilk man thay war woud ſpeid rout irkſum labouring lang ſtremes welis round ſwirlyng ouer ſlyding faſt vpwartis ryuere hid ouerheildit mony treis ſere endlang ſtyll fludis calme bene thay ſeik ſchere throw woddis grene eneas kyng euander met bandis kyndnes betuix thame knet fyry ſon aſcendit eum myddil warld regioun heuin know myd day quhen fer ciete wallis ſe thay • wris hous hedis raw skatterit diſpers bot ane knaw quhilk mychty power rome town vnto heuin mad equale renowne king euander noblis mychty held tyme bot ſobir ſenȝeory haiſt thidder thare ſteuinnis ſtere eneas ſort toun drew nere king euander borne archade percaſe ſelf day ane grete honour maid solempnit feiſt ful hie ſacrifice vnto grete hercules thare gyſe foſter ſon vnto amphitrion vthir goddis euery one ciete ane hallowit fchaw pallas ſon thidder alſo draw togidder principallis ȝounkeris ſobir ſenatouris pure officiaris ſamyn keſt enſence ane ſtew beſyde altare blude ſ • hed ſkalit new beand lew warme thare fulfaſt reik bot ȝit al ſwyth thay perſauit eik grete bargis ſlidand thus raw throw derne woddis faſt thidder draw ſtilly bendand vp thare airis ilk wicht thay wourth affrayit ſuddane ſycht euery man thay left burdis hye fute gan ſterting maniorie quhen hardy pallas forebyd defend thare ſacrifice brek quhil war end hynt ane wappin ane menȝe thaym recounter anone furth haldis ȝit wele fer ane hil ane know thaym callis ſtandȝing men quhat caus mouit ȝoupallas oracione troiās apoun ſic way thir ſtrang wentis vnknawin aſſay quhidder etil ȝe quhat kinrent ȝe schaw quhens ȝe come quhilk ȝour countre quhidder ȝe bring vnto oure boundis boidworde peaceeneas anſwere cummys fere eneas tho fader wourſchip maid anſuere fra pulpit ſchip hand ſtraucht furth mycht ſe takin pece ane branche oliue tre freynd quod thou ſeis pepil troy latyne folkis enemyis man boy quhilk flemyt realme newly agane thay ilk latynis ſocht wyth proude bergane vnto king euander al ſeik require ſuccours ſupple bare meſſage declare plane choſin men diſcend king dardane bene hidder cummyn beſeking freyndſchip knyt vp band armes fallouſchip pallas aſtoniſt ſa hie ane name dardanus abaſit worth ſchame cum furth quod quhat euer thou berne bald ſay fader quhat thou wald enter lugeing reſt quhare thou ſal reſſauit welcum geſt furth anone hynt hym hand ane wele lang quhile rycht arme embraſand syne furth togidder rakit thay raw flude thay leif enteris ſchaw eneas tho freyndly commonyng spake curteſlye thus ſayand kyng thou maiſt curteseneas oration euander king deſyryng helpe prince beſt nede euer byget grekis ſede quham fortonn wald ſuld cummin lawlie beſekin requere wald alſo ſuld furth reik wippit bendis branche oliue tre takin thy ſupple nede forſoith caucht maner fere drede thocht thou ane capitane grekis yborne alſo archade cuntre blude conionit athrides tway meane agamenone menelay bot myne aum vertew haly akillis goddis diuyne myrakillis forbearis al ane kinrede thy fame diuulgate euery ſtede fermly adioynit vnto fatis eik tharto inducis wilfully obey thare commaund schir dardanus king firſt land belt cietie troy ilion cheif fader grekis grantis ilk one borne alectra atlas douchter ȝing caryit ſchip come firſt troyis ring alectra grete atlas begat ſchuldir beris heuynnis plat marcury fader ȝour clan alſua quham ſchene mayden fare freſche maye apoun froſ • hillis top al bare quhilk cillenus hate archada bare ilk maya ſoithlie gif ony credence ſe may gif atlas begat famyn atlas rollis heuynlie ſterrit cumpas baith kinrentis ſchortlie conclude diuidit ar furth ane ſtok blude quhare hauand confidence thir thingis thir ambaſſiat meſſage writingis vthir craft thy frendſchip firſt ſocht bot ſelf perſoun come vnto ſubmittit hede pray ſocht lawlie ſtede ilk pepil vnder dawnus king rutulianis gouerning quhilk ledis aganis thy cuntre cruel batel perſewis gif thay micht expel v land thay wene tharby may thaym gane ſtand bot thay ſal vnder thare ſenȝeory subdew hale thirldome italy occupy thay boundis orientale quhare ouir ſe flowis alhale eik thay weſtir partis traiſtis quhilkis bedyit nethir ſe reſſaue knit vp faith ferme cunnand tak promit gif v faith band strang bodyis til abide bargane haue haidy myndis battel melle exercit wexe expert ſic nedis luſty ȝouth liklie dedis thus ſaid eneasthe kinges gentyl anſuere eneas euander fra tyme firſt ſpeik began ene mouth al body richt gan behald eſpying wyth ſycht syne ſchortly madeofferynge hym hys help thyngis anſuere thus agane thou glaidly maiſt forcy troyane reſſaue tendir freynd fere full blyithly knaw wele may voce wordis ſpeche lei thy fader greteſt anchiſes ful perfitly draw mynd viſſage wourthy knycht maiſt kynd ful wele remember lang tyme gone pryame ſon kyng leamedone weſy ſyſteris land heſyona socht ciete hecht ſalamonya ſamyn rais vayage made throw cald froſty boundis archade grene ȝouth tyme pylis ȝing fyrſt cled chyn berd begouth ſpryng ioyit ſe tha troyane dukis ilkone ſon kyng leamedone ſay ilk ȝoung pryamus behald maruell gloryus bot thy fader anchiſes quhare went hier fer al remanent mind brynt ȝouthede throw deſyre ſpeik commun lordly ſyre acquentit ione hand tyl hand couenand knyt bynd forwart band ilkane quhilk war away tak bad bring agane ſelf troyane men fute hate ſonkis gerſy ſcheraldis doun ſet thare principale capitane ſyne enee beſyde ſelf deis reſauis benk ybeildit grene holyne wyth preſeruit fra cruell perrellus pane hantis ſeruyce apoun manere proper det obſeruance ilk ȝere fyrſt behald ȝone ſchorand henchis brow quhare ȝone craggy rochis hingis huge wechty brayis bene doun gap cacus na mare bot ſchap mannis forme ſkant halfthe tale caucus man throw cruel dedis iniquite ȝone feyndlich hol duelt allane ane hellis byke quhare ſonnys bene neuer nane quhare wyle fleure euer cacus god fyre fader vulcanus mouth ane wounder thing ſe faderiz reky flamb furth ȝeſkis body quharſo euer paſſit buſtuous ſtatur like none vthir proces tyme laſt v inſpirit ſend v help ful lang deſirit becuunnyn mychtful goddis preſence dantaris monſtouris defence maiſt redoutit hercules come hand auenture vnto ilk land new ſlauchter ſtrang melle gerioun quhilk hedis thre proude ſpulȝe arriuing triumphal conqueroure maid thidder driue cal bullus oxin huge grete eik ky paſture ete endlang ȝone wale large wyde tuk thare lugeing riuer ſyde bot vndantit furius mynde theif schrewit cacus al way myſcheif thrawart engyne ſle conſait manere wikkitnes diſſa • micht ne durſt tak hand ne vnaſſayit leif land foure ſemelie oxin body grete ſquare al mony tendir quyes excedand fare al thay cattal away draif thay tred fuld na way perſaif vnto caue ay bak wartis talis turne thare fute ſteppis thaym harlis tralis thus ſpreith vnto ane quhine ſtane cloſit gyn sic way wrocht quhay thare tred lyft goif na taikynnis ſuld conuoy thame coif mene quhyle al beiſtis war repaterit wele eftir thaire nychtis lare hercules depart hen behuffit morow airly firſt thay remouit catal gan rowting cry rare woddis rang thare ſound ouer alquhare wyth thare noyis dynnyt hyllis knowis quhilk caue ane quyok lowis wyth loud voce ſqueland gouſty hald al cacus traiſt reuylit ſcho tald bot tho greif wourthy hercules alcius neuo douchty alcydes ſo oft ſyis clepit commonly within ſkyn begouth birn fry brym furie bittir gal wappynnis armour hynt wythal wechty burdoun knorry • e hillis heicht held ane raſe firſt time ony erd pepyl perſauit cacus efferd within hede trublyt ene tuay swift wynd fled gar away caue ſped cry ſprete drede adionit wyngis foot fra ſelf ſeſit tharein ane ſtane huge wecht clois gyn lete fal ſic haiſt doun thrang chenȝeis brak quharewith feſſynnyt hang forgit war faderis engyne grete irne ſlottis ſchet entre ſyne bot lo haiſt hercules come hand furious mynd carying ouer land paſſage entre ſeking beſely ene thare rolling hie gnaſſing teith birnand full ire auentinis hill thryis ſwyre ſeſis ouer thryis aſſayis brek rent craggy ſtone entre bot thocht neuer ſo wycht thryis irkit doun hillis hicht reſt vale gone thare ſtude ane pynnakyll quhyn flynt ſtone apoun bak ſide cauerne cald rais one end rycht hie hald wilde foulis reif ane ganand ſtede rent raw fleſche beiſtis agemenon menclay ȝit allane caus armes ſteris pepyl myce moue battal weris bot pryncipally querrel myne knaw gif bene yneuch thay ſchaw thay bot ani dyſtroyit aucht war yneuch mycht ſuffice think thay haue faltit anys lang tyme quhy doubyl thay thare treſpas thocht wemen brocht thame foly ȝit hait thay wemen alutterly quhat mene thay myddil mantil wall lityl ſtop dykis fowſyis wene thay bene ane reſt eis ȝour bodyis ȝour hors quhil day bot hald ȝou reddy batal ay mene tyme nycht wache cure gif meſapus ȝettis diſcure bete brycht fyris wallis twys ſeuin rutulianis al chance befallis war choſin knychtis wache toun eik ane hundreth followis reddy boun ȝoung gallandis purpure creſtis rede thare giltin gere maid glittering euery ſtede quhar ſo thay walk rownys ſtil ſoft thay ſtalk wardis hedis thay ſtuffit al nicht fele tymes haiſty effere drede portis veſy thay gif ocht war nede draw briggis ȝettis vpraſit ioned wallis thay ſuld betraſit euery man ſtud reddy gere enarmed weil hand thaym bald ſchil froſtis wattir cald childer ȝing exercis beſelie hunting houndis horne ſchout crye wylde dere throw woddis chace mate dant ryn horſis late thare gam ſport thay hant raw wyth thare thundering ſamyn ſoundit dedely bowis ſtring quhirrand ſmertly furth flaw takyll tyte qwite throw hede remulus ſmyte groundin ſteile throw templis glaid hald thy wayis haiſt aſcaneus ſaid thy ſelf boundis lyte ſayand thus hie heuin al tyte diſcendis mouand haleſum chyld aſcaneus ſocht richt thare figure changeit tyme wald likenes ane butes hare ald purſeuant fore ſquyare troiane anchyſes fader ſtede ſtrang numanus thou doung dede fyrſt louyng eik hie renowne ſouerane appollo grantis nane diſdene ſall haue ſoithly perigall archery leif chylde ſyc batell ceis na mare tyme draw preis wyſe carpis brycht appollo myddis ſermond tho waniſt fer away wat neuer quhare furth mortall ſycht ſchyre nobyllis troyanis capitanis trew thir taikynnis god appollo knew hard arrowis clatterand caſe tharfore thay haue withdraw furth place aſcaneus brycht phebus mychty targe wald na langare thole hym go large thocht fecht deſyre ioy name tyl hys innis thay conuoy syne bargane thame ſped agane ſchaw big ȝoung men thay war ſo grete wicht equale ſemyt thame hicht fir treis thare landis hillis thare eik ſa egir thare willis thay porte quhilk eneas charge commandit ſteikit large warpit opin dyntis rude quhil fleis lap flude laſt mneſteus ſtrang sereſtus troiane capitanis herand thus thare pepil ſlane war doun conuene thare feris fleand pale wan haue thay ſene thare cheif inemye cloſit thare wallis mneſteus thaym clepis thus callis quhare ettill ȝe fra hynemneſteus callys agane hys troyanis fleyng quhiddir wald ȝe fle quhat vthir wallis ſeik ȝe ciete quhare haue ȝe outhir ſtrenth forteres cietezanis behaldis expres nane bot ane man ſtandand ȝou aganis cloſit within ȝour dykis wallis ſtanis vnreuengit ſo grete occiſioun huge ſlauchter ſal mak within ȝour toun ſa feil vailȝeand ȝoung capitanis kend vnreſiſtit thus doun hell ſal ſend maiſt vnwourthy cowartis ful ſleuth ȝour vnſilly cuntre haue ȝe na reuth piete ȝour ancient goddis kind think na lak ſchame ȝour mynd ſa grete outrage ſtrang enee obſence thus catifely fle troyanis ſic wourdis ſaid curage grew fermlie al abaide thare famen flokkand ane rout turnus ane litil thocht ſtark ſtout begouth frawart bargane draw ſattil towartis riuer ſyde law aye pece pece part toun cloſit riuer rynnand doun troianis ſeand mare apertly aſſailȝeit mony ſchout cry thikkit faſt inuiroun quhen awful wylde lyoun wyth thare inuaſibil wappinnis ſcharp ſquare ane multitude men belappit war ful feirs thrawin vult ſtart seand ſcharp poyntis reculis bak wart bot gif bak fle away nouthir greif curage ſuffer may thocht wald al mekil mycht aganis ſo mony men wappinnis bricht preis fordward may cum na ſpede nane vthir turnus ſic ane nede steppis abak huly pay ful ſtil mynd ſkaldand greif egir wil ferder eik amyd feris twyis ſtrenth mycht iupiter heuynnis fare send doun iris quhilk duellis vnto ſpous ſiſter thare hand ful ſcharp chargis bringis command le thare turnus euer chance befallis withdraw fra fatal troiane wallis quharthrow vailȝeand campyone ȝoung kene nowthir ſcheild ſameikle mycht ſuſtene ſic defence make hand wyth dartis hym ſchakkit thare ſic wyſe quhelmyt confoundit euer ane bos helme rang ſoundit clynkand halffettis ane dyn ſouir armour ſtrang nathyng thyn brokin birſit fele ſtanis caſt thik war dyntis ſtrakis ſmyte ſa faſt helme doun beting war creiſtis sa ſare boſis terget preſt ſcheild mycht langar ſic routis ſuſtene troianis mneſteus thare tene doublis thare dyntis wyth ſperis caſt bene hidduous thunderis blaſt ouer al body furth ȝet ſwete thik lyke trynland blak ſtremes pik ne gat laſare anys aynd draw f • blit breith ful faſt bete blaw amyd wery breiſt lymmes laſche laſt al ſuddanly ane plaſche harnes al togiddir quhare ſtude ſelf ſwakkis lap flude giltyn ſtremes keppit riuere bare vp aboue thir wallis clere syne blyithlye cariit feris bedene blude ſlauther away weſchyn cl • ne finis prologe x booke hie plaſmatour thyngis vniuerſal thou reneware kyndin thys prolog ſchawis god workes incomprehenſybil mānis wit reaſon preuis creacyon myſtery trinite creat al incomprehenſibil thy werkis ar conſaif quhilk grantit euery wicht haif quhat thing maiſt ganis vnto gouernale quhow meruellus bene diuiſiouns thy gracis diſtribute ſo ilk thing al placis ſon ſchyne ouer al ſchaw licht day labour reſt thou ordanit nicht diuers cauſis ſchupe ſere ſeſſouns ſpacis freſche vere burgioun herbis ſueit flouris hate ſomer nuris corne al houri brede al kynd foulis fyſche beiſt heruiſt rendir frutis maiſt leiſt wyntir ſnyb erth wyth froſty ſchouris thocht thou nedit al thing thou furth hede eneas ſamyn ſtede kneis grippit humelie pietuous voce ſyne thus begout cry thy dere faderis goiſt beſeik gude beleif quhilk thou eik aſcaneus vpriſing eſtate ſilly ſaul myne ſa faynt mate thou ſauf myne awne ſon fader dere haue houſe riche full mobillis ſere quharin bedeluin lyis ane grete talent charge fyne ſiluer veſchell quent forgeit pounſit wounder craftely ane huge wecht fyneſt gold tharby vncunȝete ȝit ne neuir put werk sa thou ſaif thy piſſance ſa ſtark troianis glorie thare victorye sall na thing change dymynew tharby ane pure ſaule thus hingand ballance may ſic diuiſioun mak diſcrepance thus ſaid ſilly magus vane quham enease • ea anſwere anſweris thus agane thy mony talentis fyne ſiluer gold quhilkis thou reherſand tald keip vnto thy ſmall childer airis late thame belouit moder ſall haue erd cuſtome delf graif na thy bone honour ſyc cure thame lay faderis ſepulture bot ſall left wylde beiſtis fude ſpate wattir flude sall bere depe thareon raw emptiue throttis ſall thy banis gnaw thir ſey monſtouris thare wod rage lape thy blude thare hunger aſſuge syne delay antheus licas quhhilkis turnus firſt warde ladaris perſewis alſo neuma bold camerthes brycht ſpere forganis thame ſicht appere quham ligere carpis apoun hie thou ſeis diomedis ſtedis ſaid ȝit achilles chare perſauis draw thocht athir vniqueſt feild knaw ȝit troiane planis behaldis thou end thy age bargane sall maid thir landis ground sic wourdis vane vn ſemelie ſound furth warpis wyde ligere fulichelie bot troiane baroun vnabaſitlie na wourdis pres render agane bot fa let fle ane dart flame hit lutagus quhilk fra felt dynt ſchaft hinging ſcheild ſtynt bad driue hors char al fordwert ſtreicht addreſt feicht ſtrekit furth left fute chare bot ſone eneas ſpere reddy beneth ſchynand ſcheild 〈◊〉 law grundyn hede ilk thraw left flank liſk perfit tyte quhill clare ouer chariot ſinyte ground weltis dede thrawis quhom wiſe ſoure wordis ſawis pieteous eneas begouth ſchyde lutagus ſayd forſoith tyde na ſlaw cours thy hors weldy thy carte rendrit thy inemye ȝit nane vane wrinchis gaiſtis quent thy chare conſtrenit bakwart went magre thyne wythdraw fais grippis lo thy fre wyll thou ſkippis ouer quhelis thy carte god wa • leiffand renȝeis hors al deſolate beand ſaid hors renȝeis hynt tothir fey bruthir euer ſtynt lap fra cart lurkand pieteouſly vp heuand bare handis thus dyd cry troyane prynce lawly beſeik thyneawne vertuisa humbyl ſupplication thewis meik thy parentis maiſt renowne ſyc ane child engendrit thou ſpare ſylly wofull ſaul leyſt haue reuth admyt requeſt wyth wourdis fele thus gan requere enee laſt wyſe made anſuere syc ſawis war langayr thy mynde sterff behuffis le thou war vnkynd leif thy brother deſolate hym allane na fallow ſamyn gate tharewych hirnys leif dere thyne opinioun diſſauit thou beleiffit may thou ſe venus doi ſuſtene fortyfye thy troyane routis puſſance nane actiue handis ſtout myndis mene bodyis reddy perrell ſuſtene haue thay thou may ſe experience quham iuno wyth humyle reuerence anſueri • ſueit maiſt gudlie huſband quhare liſt renew ſorow hand careful wycht lykis ſyc bourdis efferit thy fatall dredefull wourdis beſtad bot war wene al ſtrangly belouit ſumtyme haue bene thocht ȝit god wa • e accordit ſo baith honour thy dignite ſay war belouit thou ioue almychty rengand euermare suld deny ſo ſobir ane thyng bot mycht withdraw lyking furth feyld turnus ſaif vnto fader dawnus ouer laif belouit hym reſſoun wald quod ſche ſal periſche ſal de ſched gentyl blude ſo pacient greuous panys troianis tort rent neuer le kyn wourſchip thy mychtye maieſte ſouerane king heuyn etheriall wourdis maid anſure thus al gif thou aſkis reſpit delay bot ane tyme till ane certane day thys euident deith turnus ȝing deſiring ſuld grant 〈◊〉 tyme quhilk grant quod bot gif ſa beis vnder thy requeiſt mare hie pardoun lurkis wald thou ceiſt gif thou wenys al victorye batall chancis may reducit alterit clare agane ane myſbeleue thou foſteris al vane quham iuno wyſe ſayd wepyng quhat harme mycht fall thocht ſum takin ſing thow ſchew thy mynd grantit quod ſche quhilk wourdis fatal deſtany grounſchis thou gif concede ſay quhat force thocht thou dede woldeſt repreif ratyfy agane turnus lyffe ane lang tyme ſuld remane bot approchis innocent knycht ane fereful end ſal dede dycht ſawis ar voyde verite wald god rather ſo ſuld diſſauit war bot fals drede thou liſt thou mycht dede thy fatal promyſſis thy ſtatutis ſtrange bettir purpois tranſlate change fra ſche thir wourdis ſayd ilk tide doun heuin ſche lete hir ſelfin •• yde driuand ane tempeſtuous wynd al eik behynd within ane cloude myſt circulit clene sche throw bownit furth thys quene towart troyane oiſtis planys tentis ſocht laurentanis goddes furth ane bois cloude liknes thareto eikis ſche euery ſtede quent fenȝeit wourdis faynt counterfete voce mynd ony vthir conſate fenȝeis eik hir counterfete paſis sic lik thay ſay diuers placis wrachis walkis goiſtis ar dede ſlepy dremes fra ſtede ſtede fleand ſweuyn makis illuſiouns quhen mennys mynd oft driuylling gronys forefront feild rycht haltanlie curagious vnder ſcheild muſturis thys ymage wyth dartis kene aggreuit turnus child 〈◊〉 prouocand bargane ire turnus tho al hate fire figure inuade thare grete diſpite ane quhirland dart let fle bot ilk ſchaddow ſum dele addred turnit gaif bak fled turnus wenyng enee tane flycht awounderit ſelcouth ſycht wythin hys mynd ane vane comfort caucht cryis loude quhiddir fleis thou enee leif neuer ſchame thus deſolate waiſt thy new alliance promiſt haiſt lauinia ſpouſinge chalmer hand al ilk regioun land quhilk thou ſafer ſoucht ouer ſe richt hand ſal ſauyn gif quod ſic wourdis ſchoutand perſew ay glymmerand brand ſchuke ſchew na thyng perſauand myrth blis away quyte wynd bewaffit cais thare ſtude ane meikle ſchip tyde hir wail ioned til ane ſthore rolkis ſyde wyth plankis wyth briggis laid land entre reddy graithit wele thay fand quhilk ſchip oſynus king wy come laitely ciete cluſis thiddir went wrayth ſchado enee ſemyt abaſit faſt fle hid hir derne vnder hichis therin na ſlaware turnus haiſtis hym ryn delay ſpedis ſchip ran ouer brig inwyth burd ſkip ſkars enterit fore caſtell quhen ſaturnus douchter ſaw hir tyme befell ſone cabyl ſonder ſmitis ſche fra ſchore draif ſchip throw ſe bot turnus abſent thus ſamyn houre eneas ſerchis throw amyd ſtoure renk quham euer met lay dede full mony ane man kelit ſtede tharewyth lycht fenȝeit goiſt fra tyme ſchyp chargit fra coiſt na langer ſekis hirnes hyr hyde bot flew vp ſamyn tyde deſoluit ane dyrk cloud mene ſeſſoun force wyndis loud turuus fer furth amid depe ſe dryue dyd behald tho belyue ignorant quhat wyſe thys chance wrocht hys lyffe ſauyng nothing roucht wyth handis ioned vp towartis heuyn sic wourdis furth brade wyth drery ſteuin almychty faderturnus oracion iupiter heuinnys hye thou reput ſic wyſe confuſit ſchame myne offence wyl ſuffir ſic torment penance quhidder driue quhens cummyn quhat maner eſchewing fleing haue mummyn quhat eſtate ſall returne agane sall neuir ſe wallis laurentane euir eſt tentis ſall ſe quhat may ȝone oiſt men ſay quhilkys querrel followit feild quhom allace fethtand vnder ſcheild ȝounder ſchame ſay harme ſo wikkitly reddy myſchevus deith beleft haue lo behald thaym fleand pail wan heris granyng mony douchty man defalt falland fey ground quhat ſal allace woful ſtound quhilk land thocht ane thouſand tymes ſteruit may ſwelly ſo depe haue ſeruit bot ȝe wyndis rather haif mercy rolkis craggis ſwak ſchip ſen na erth ſe haue wrechit turnus ſum piete quhil hys fre wil ſtad manere beſeikis ȝou al hart • te prayer warp body ſchald vnkend fer furth cirtis warldis end quhare rutulianis neuer fynd agane sa fame rumoure may remane efter deith thik hale ſchoure ſchaftis ſchutis bot lyke ane ferme rolk quhilk ſe screkyt lench amid large ſe situate agane rageand wyndis blaſt brym wallis boldynnand wounder faſt violence doi hym ſelf defend palynus eik accuſtumate fle bot wyth ane ſtane licagus britnythe quhilk afane montane ſemetane grete nuke quhom viſage ouertuke palynus • och sennouns ſmate tway made ſa ſlaw mycht fle away thare armour ſyne lauſus geuin ſulderis croun hie creſtis ſet quhylk ſo rychely ſchane ſlew alſo euancus ane troiane myna ſyne kelis feild quhilum parys companȝeone ane euin eild quham one ane nycht theana gude fare hys fader amytus troy bare quhen hecuba douchter ciſſeus dremyt ſche grete ſtory telly thus wyth ane fyre brand ſelf nycht deliuer paris fey knycht quhilk natyue ciete maid end bot thare feildis laurentyne vnkend haldis body myna brym ſtoure ſtound mezentius like ſtrenthy ſanglerea compariſon bore quham houndis queſt mony quhryne rore doun driuing hychtis made deſcend quhilk mony clamour infeſtis tyde vnabaſit euery ſyde behaldis girnand ful propir tene ſcheild choppit ſchaftis bedene furth ancient boundis chorit tho cumming ane greik quhilk clepit arto fugitiue luſty hete ane hungry lyoun rummiſſing conſtrenit hys empty rageand maw beiſtis dennys circuland al raw gif cais eſpies ane ſwyft ra ȝoung hart ſpringand tyndis twa ioyfull bradis theron diſpituuſly wyth gapeand rout ruſchyt hye doun ſmytis fey atroun amyd oiſt ded thraw ȝaldand vp goiſt smate wyth hys helys ground matalent brokin ſchaftis wyth hys blude byſprent thys ilk mezentius eik dedenȝete toſla orodes quhilk flocht knaw quhylk frawart went repute na wyſe hys entent sic ſteand wound hys bake vnwarniſt quhen na defence micht make bot ran met hys rais athir man aſſemblit face face orodes prettik mare al bot tothir dedis armes mare ſtout erth ouerthrawin fere poſſand hym wyth ſtalwart ſpere apoun ſet fute thus ſayd feris beis baith blyith glaid lo ane grete partye lei lyis erde douchty orodes feris ſamyn raſit vp ane cry wyth ioyus ſound ſygne victory blew priſe triumphale deith bot orodes ȝeldand vp breith vnto mezentius carpis thus hye vnreuengit thou ſall neuir victor wele wate ſone ſal wrokin na al thy proude wourdis thou ſpokin thou ſal endure ſyc ioy bot ſiclyke chancis ſembland ennoy abidis thocht thou neuir ſa bald ſamyn feild ſall thy dede corp withhald quham mezentius ſmyland ſayd tene thou ſal de firſt quhat euer foreſene prouidit almychty ioue quod quham fader goddis king men clepe ſayand thus ſchaft ilk thraw furth wound body draw orodes hard reiſt doi oppres cald irny al buſtuous hidduous orion quhen fu • e wod throw mekylſe scherand ſtreme ſchuldderis hie aboue wallis flude apperis like ane anciant aik tre mony ȝeris grew apoun ſum mountane • oppis hycht semand ſo hie euery mannis ſicht quhilk thocht rutis ſprede ground ſydis crop vpſtracht amyd cloudis hydis siclike mezentius muſturis feild wyth huge armour baith ſpere helme ſcheild aganis quham eneas faſt hyis fra tyme amyd rout hym eſpyis tothir vnabaſit al reddy thare cummyng douchty aduerſare abydis ſtoutly fermyt force maſſalie vpſtude wyth buſtuous cors meſurand hys e al large ſpayis mycht thraw ane caſting ſpere thus ſayis rycht hand fleand dart mot quhilk cais verray▪ god aſſiſtyng ſchot beſeik awow promittis eik ſing trophe triumphale meith louyt ſon lauſus cleith ſpulȝe al harnes rent quod ȝounder rubaris body fals enee thus ſayd fra hand ilk tyde caſting dart faſt birrand lattis glyde fleand ſtlentis eneas ſcheild syne ſtaudand fer roume ȝonde feild smat wourthy achores ilk thraw betuix bowellis ribbis law anthores ane grete hercules feris come arge luſty ȝeris inherdand euander arthade duellyng reſidence made palentyne ciete italiane vnhappely liggis thus doun ſlane ane wound dynt within fycht addre • ſſit towart ane vthir mycht deand beheld heuynnys large behald ſwete cuntre arge reuthful eneas keſt ſpere quhilk throw mezentius armour dyd ſchere throucht gird arge platit thryis wyth ſtele throw co • chit lynnyng euery dele thrynfald playis bullis hydis law doun flank dynt abydis bot bereft nowthir lyffe ne mycht eneas quhilk expert ficht ioyfull quhen mezentius blud ſaw furth hynt hys ſwerd hang law feruently towart hys fa pa quhilk dynt ſum dele aſtoniſt quhen lawſus ſaw auenture wepit wale ſare hys fader dere wo begone become thys luſty man ſalt teris faſt ouer hys chekis ran forſoith ſal ouer ſlip ſtede thy hard myſchance lauſus fatale dede thy mayſt douchty actis bellical freſche ȝoungkere maiſt ding memorial ſal rehers gif ony fayth may geuin ſa grete dedis antiquite mezentius menȝeit drew abak harland leg quharin ſchaft ſtak quhare went beris ouer feild hys inemyis lance faſt fixit ſcheild betuix thaym ruſchis ȝoung lawſus amyd thare wappinnis ſterne curageus ſelf ſet ſuſtene fycht vnder eneas richt hand raſit hycht reddy ſmyte ane dedely wound inſteppis baldlie ilk ſtound bytand brand vpheuit keppit reſiſt ſtent grete ene feris followis ane felloun ſchout quhil mezentius feild wan defend couerit ſonnys ſcheild thay caſt dartis thikfald thare lord heild wyth ſchaf • ſchot flanys grete plente perturband thare feirs aduerſare enee al enragit ſouir targe erekkit thare vnder hym haldis cloiſly dekkit lyke ſum tyme cloudisa compariſon briſtis attanis ſchoure furthȝettand hoppand haleſtanys al plowman thare hynes hy fleis croftis feildis eik trauelloure ȝound vnder wald lur kand withdrawys ſum ſouir hald owthir vnder wattir brayis bankis dern ſum craggis clift depe cauerne lang ſchoure leſtis plane may quhen ſon ſchynes agane exerce hys iournay werk al faſt siclike ene wyth ſchot dartis caſt ouer held vnbeſet ilk ſyde quhill preis batall ſtyntis tyde al thare force ſuſtenit deray repreuand lawſus thus begouth ſay mannyſand wyth brand blude rede quhiddir haiſtis thou ſa faſt apoun thy dede quhow dar thou vndertak ficht syc interpryſe quhilk aboue thy micht thou art wiſe thy tendir hart quod reuthfull mynd diſſauis bot al hait blude sone eftir ſpret lyffe furth went doun goiſtis law ſad entent left body dede hyne dyd pa bot quhen anchiſes ſon feirs eneas beheld vult contenance deing ſwete viſſage ſua dede thrawyng becummyn wan pale dyuers wyſe ſychit profoundlye owthir twis thryis draif abak hys hand reuch hynt ſa mynd eftir dynt ymage hys faderly piete emprentit that▪ wiſe ſaid doughty ȝinglyng wourthy menit wourthy bewallit complenit quhat ſal reuthful compacient enee ſa grete louabil dedis render quhat may ȝelde ſufficient ſic naturale inborne hardyment thyne armour quharof ſum tyme thou reioſit leif ay enioſit vnto thy parentis handis ſepultre beleif entirit quod gyf ſic manere tryumphe coiſt may thame pleſure elli thy goiſt bot thou vncilly chyld ſa wyll rede counfort wyth thy lamentabyl dede thou ouer machit art thus lyis ſlane greteſt eneas handis twane syne feris repreif chyde thay ſa lang delayit beſyde makand na haiſt bere corp away ſelf betuix handis tway dede body vp lyftis fra ground rede blude new grene wound beſparkit ȝallow lokkis brycht ayre kemmyt addreſſit rycht ¶ fra mezentius knew ȝoung lauſus decei • reuenge lyfe loiſt pr • mene ſeſſoun fader feris doun flude ſyde tyberis stanchit woundis water weſchand ſwete blude body helme ſtele beſyde hang wele ne apoun ane grane branche ane grene tre vthir wechty harnes gude nede lay gers beſyde hym mede crafty choſen verlottis ful ſore woundit dout stude lenand wery nek bonis ouer ane bowand tre wyth ſary grones hys wele kemmyt berde hingand doun ful ſtraucht vpon breiſt vntil girdil raucht fele tymes lauſus menys prayand ful oft micht ſaufelie ſe mony meſſengeris vnto ſend wythdraw hym feild defend abyde na langare bargane ſchaw hym quhat ſorow fader tane bot lauſus dede▪ feild hys woful feris caryit apoun ane ſcheild wepand ſa grete ane man brocht ground diſco • feſt wyth ſa griſlie ane wound mezentius mynd conſait ilk tyde suſpekand harmes quhilkis war tho betyde fer conſiderit caus thare murnyng canois hare duſt ſlyng mekil pouder fylland haſart hede baith handis ſamyn ſtede towart heuin vpheuis ane fary goddis ſternes faſt wary syne lenand ſonnis corp thus cryis dere chyld tender get heir lyis ſa grete appetitemtzētius lamentis ſonnis dede delyte vnto wrechit lyfe ſa ful ofſyte ſufferit entir ony ſtede vnder fay handis thy dede lyfe ſalſit ſa thy fader quhilk begat onely ſon ſo dere suld ſaif leiffand eftir throw thay ſa griſly woundis ſe allace vnto wrechit catyue thyng myne exile laſt bannaſſyng becummyn hard vnſufferabil ſtound deith panys lamentabil depe ingrauyn myne hart vnſound ſmytyn wyth mortal wound ſelf man caus thy dede wyth treſpas chyld euery ſtede filit glore honour thy name thy hie renowne beſpottand wyth ſchame inuy haitrent myne awne pepil thare hale aſſent expellit ſceptre ryng addettit miſdoing vnto cuntre haue ſufferit pane aucht wourthy haue bene flane hane ȝeld wikkit ſaul myne maner torment pyne till amend offence feid ha leif allace thou art dede ȝit want men cumpany nouthir licht lyffe clerenes ſkye bot ſone ſall thame leif part therfra ſayand thus ſamyn mynd full thra raſit vp apoun woundit determyt reuenge de thocht violence ſare ſmert maid vnfery ȝit ſtalwart hert curage vndekyit gude innede bad ga fethe rhebus riall ſtede quhilk wourſchip comfort hale ſupport fais till aſſale hors euery grete iourney hame fra feild victor eſchapitt quham mezentius ony mare abayde seand ſted droupand ſad thus ſayd rhebus twa le • fit lang yfere gif mortall wichtis erde ony tyme may reput lang quod outhir day beis thou reuengit lauſus dolorus deith wreik ſchame ſall v victor bringin hame ȝone bludy ſpulȝe eneas hede gif na ſtrenth force ſtede ſuffar ony way ſo ſal feild ſamyn de baith two thou moiſt forcy ſtede louit fole wiſe beleif thou may tho • e ony vtheris commandment leiſt dedenete gif war ſchent tyl obey ony maiſter lord troiane ſay thus ful cowartlie anone ſtede bekend held ſchoulder plat eis vpon bak doun ſat baith handis fillit dartis kene helme hede birniſt bricht ſchene bone quhilk tymbret buklit lyke til ane lokkerit mane mony fa ſic array ſwift cours furth ſteris ſtede draif melle depe hart boldynnys felloun mycht ouercum deſtroy ſen haif tynt warldly ioy nowthir abhor dede ſterue fecht rek ocht ony goddis mycht deſyſt ceis boiſt mannace cummin de ilk place bot fyrſt bryng thir rewardis quod wyth word fa ane dart lete fle eftir ane vthir caſt ſyne ane vthir fixit faſt hym prekand ane cumpas large bot al thir dintis ſufferit goldin targe thryiſe left half faſt weir woud eneas rade quhare ſtude thyk wyth handis ſwakkand dartis kene thryis troiane prince ouer al grene tyl ſtalwart ſtelit ſcheild ſtekand lyke ane hare wod dartis bare laſt ennoyit thys deray irkſum traſing iowking delay commerit wox ſa mony dartis vane thus oft draw furth caſt agane machit time fale wyth hys fa men bargane inequale quhilk ay ane auantage flocht full mony thyngis reuolwit thocht syne man ruſchit tene forehede betuix horſys ene keſt ſpere al force mycht vpſtendit ſtalwart ſtede one hicht helis flang vp doun ſwakkis knycht ſone wyth ane felloun fare founderis fordwart flatlingis ſpald ouerquhelmyt man hys feyld vnfald latynis eik pepil troianis heuynnis dynlyt ane ſchout atanis eneas gird aboue ane braide hynt furt ſwerd forther thus ſaide quhare mezentius ſa ſterne quhare ſtout feirs curage berne quham mezentius ilk prince tyrrhene fra mycht alifting vp ene ſe heuynnys lycht draw breith richt mynd agane recouerit haith thus anſwerismezentius laſt anſeuer afor decht thou diſpitefull fo quharto chydis thou reprochand ſo mannaſſis dede ſlanchter thinke na velany ſic wiſe come feild ſtand aw ſwelt vnder ſcheild beleif na freyndſchip thy handis nane ſic trety ſauthning commandis ſon lauſus band vp perfay bot ane thing beſeik pray gif ony pleſure may grantit beild till aduerſaris lyis vincuſt feild knaw ſuffir body haue ane ſpulture erd graue knaw ſtandand ſtede folkis bitter haitrent grete feid defend thare furour requere grant corp beſyde ſonnys fere ſum tumbe entirit ſayand thus knawand muſt de ene perſauit birniſt brand throu gorgeit went eneas hand within armour ſchortlie conclude strang fortitude quhilk hardyment clepe aboue quhilk vertew ſouerane ac • ording princis heich magnanymyte ane boet ſetfort • tud ful hardenes towar • ne betuix vice twane quhame fule hardines clepit tane vndertakis al perrillis auyſe tothir namyt ſchamefull cowardiſe voyde curage dolf ony ſtane firſt hardy meſure tyme reſoun geuis na cure dout caſtis bot thinkis ſure nocht may ſuffir hete indure tothir proues ſa pure euer ſtandis fere felloun dred neuir dar vndertak ane douchty dede bot doi curage manhede ſamyn ſmure firſt ſoundis towart vertew ſum dele hardy couth auiſit hardyment tothir na forefrount quhay ſal wyn croun mede ſay euerlaſtand blys fyre eternale nedelinges moiſt thay drede criſt goſpell ſayiſ wi quha bydis contrar gif thou aganis god art thou wageour vnto lucifere god ſaue debate reuel til vertew gudnes fleſche debatis aganis ſpiritual goiſt hie curage ſenſuall luſt law body vyctor baith loſt ſprete wald vp cors ay doun liſt draw ſecound fa warld ane vthir thraw makis ſtrang aſſaltis couatice eſtate aganis quham ful perrellus debate fais familiare bene full quent knaw leif thy fleſche maiſter thy cors leif warld ay remane reſiſt freyndis ſlicht al thy force ancient enemy werſt ane ane thouſand wilis mony ane trane kendillis oft fleſche birnand hete cauſit wrechit pleſance ſem ful ſwete nocht fals warld makis fane thy fa aduerſare principale promyſſioun wald ſaul bocht aye vnto wourd thy mynd bent fele bene thy fais fers ful ſlicht bot thou ſtal wart campioun knycht feild grace foreſaid armour bricht thay mayd de bait thame lithlie ilk ficht fre thine actioun ſa wicht nane may peirs thou reſiſt ſtande becum thou towart crawdoun recriand conſent cry cok thy dede dicht think fa waik impotent may vincus nane bot thame liſt ouercum ſall neuer ouerſet thy conſent eith defence ſay na dum thy wele lo ſnm conſent neuir thou ſal neuir loiſt diſaſſent thou may vincuſt ane hoiſt ani ȝa tyne thy mede euery crun • na wounder forby exemplecompariſone ſe ſuld wyth enee bot fled fer frawart held ay withand hir cartis cours ane vthir way na le haiſt eneas bent quhelis turnis writhis mony ane went men ſeirſis throw effcayit routis callis loude cry ſchoutis al feil ſyis ene keſt apoun fa tymes hym addreſt chace ſwift cours throw melle hors ſemyt ryn foule doi fle bot euer al oft iuturna ane vthir art awaywart turnis writhis hir brotheris cart thus eneas temanys al flocht ſundry motioun ire bot al nocht allace ne knawis quhat dyuers thochtis ſere conſatis lo hys mynd mony contrare purpois ſent thus trublit entent meſapus cais nere hand left neif haldys reddy twa ſoupil caſtyug ſperis hedit wyth ſtele quham ane ful ſouirlie wele towart enee addreſſit dyd glyde eneas houit ſtil ſchot abyde hym ſchroudand vnder hys armour ſcheild bowand hoch ſtude lytle heild netheles ſpere ſcharplie ſchare baſnyt tymbrell quyte doun bare ſmate away crei •• y toppis hie mare greif ire vpgrowys seand caucht wyth diſſate ſtycht quhen perſauit hys ſycht turnus hors furth dreuinane vthir art awaywart turnis ſa feyl ſyis cart tho mony tymes loud teſtifye grete iupiter ſa wranguſty •• urit conſtrenit ficht witnes drew al grete vnrycht altaris confederance vyolate laſt ful furius hate mydwart inemyis inuaid wyth proſper chance batal ſo vnglaid terribil fais waxis hale ony difference degre wraik na man lyſt ſpare ane cruel ſ • auchter raſit thare kynd wraith breithfull yre hie lete ſlip large brydil wyth renȝe fre ¶ followis ſlauchter mouy • ald made turnus eneas hald qvhat god ſal teaching • ndy • e sa mony woundis careful ſyte quha lerne matir declare sa feil diuers ſlauchteris war thare grete deſeis dukis ſtede ouer field ſtrowin liggis dede quham euery ane ſamyn cours abut doun bet turnus eneas ſtout iupiter pleſand wyth ſa grete motiounexclamator gret ſlauchter followinge oh crudelite athir pepill ſuld ruſche vthir preis quhilkis eftir ſuld ane eterne pei eneas fyrſt taryit lang smate ane sutrone ane rutuliane ſtrang ane greuous wound hit ſyde throwout rybbis ſtyff ſwerd glyde p • irſit hys coiſt breiſtis condict hy thare fatell deith maiſt haiſty bargane firſt fermyt troyanis ſtand langeir fled turnus fra hand hand tho turnus recounterit preis amytus brother diores quham fra thare hors ground doun bet fute feild ſtrangly vmbeſet formeſt ane lang ſtyff ſpere smate dede ane ſwerd tothir fere sine baith thare hedis hakkit hy hys cart hyngis thame blude tharfra droppand turſys away theſelf ſtede eneas ane alſay ane vnſet kelit ianaus talon alſo ſtout cethegus syne eftir thame kelit preis ſa ay ſorowfull onytes renowned thebis blude ofſpryng deſcenbyng doun etheon kyng moder born peridium vther chif captane turnus kelit twa brethir war lithia ſend appollois cuntre troianis defend eftir thaym ane meneit ſlane ane ȝoung man borne archadane al dayis euir hatit melle bot al forhe moiſt nedis thus de laik larne fludis gray craft fiſching euery day ane pure cote hous held bure law rewardis riche folkis war hym vnknaw fader erit ſew ane pece feild hire gang held hys beild like fyre war vp bet ſum dry widderit wod vpſet baith thare diuers partis ſere amyd ſoundand buſkis laurere quhare fomy riueris rede ſpate hurlis doun mouth ane large gate hidduous brute felloun farde attanis thare thay rin ouer flowand al planis ilkane diſtroyis waiſtis driuis away na ſtawar bayth turnus enee hurllis ruſchis feirs throw melle nowthe great hate betuex turnus ene braithful ire felloun thocht within thare myndis boldynnys al flocht thay breiſtis na wy vincuſt breiſtis ful grief cruelte laſch thay bludy ſwerdis bricht mak woundis wyde al thare mycht tane thaym knaw enee kyng murranus anceſtry mayſt hie soundand name forefaderis auld ouer al clan latyne kyngis bald obſeruit man • e man vnto day furth carte ſmittin qwite away bet doun vnto erd wynd flaucht wyth ane grete rouk quhirland ſtane ouer raucht murranus renis chetis quherewith ſtedis ȝok kit war thretis vnder quhelis weltit doun quhare liggis morrall ſoun awne • ledis aboue rap rap ſterand hufis ſtampand mony clap ouer treddis doun thringis thare maiſter law thare lordis hi • eſtate miſknaw ane turnus recounterit ane hilo ruſchand hurllit thro melle tho full feirs mynd auſterne curage bot turnus al vaſſallage gilt halffettis ane grundin dart thraw fixt throw helme ſchaft flaw peirſand brane quhil bruſchit blude thy richt hand creteus ſa gude thou forcieſt greik cummyng fra archade land micht deliuer ilk turnus hand goddis cupentus plane mycht enee come agane bot breiſt ſteill poynt met thirlit throw doun bet nowthir ſcheild obſtant plait ſteil catiuis breiſt helpit neuir ane dele eoline feildis lawrentane behald ron doun bet ſlane thy brade bak riche wede ground thou beſpred richt fer brede thare lyis dede houſſis 〈◊〉 nobyl ſtede kynrent ſtant vndermont ida grete ciete li • neſia bot feildis laurentine ſulȝe thy ſepulture made ay apoun wyſe oiſtis wardis hale athir part returnyt batale aganis vtheris fycht ſamyn attanis latinis alhale troyanis duke mneſtheus ſterne sereſ • u tothir half prince meſapus grete horſſis danter clepit eik ſtalwar aſilas thirrene routis ſemblit attanis kyng euandrus army archadianis euery man hymſelf beſt mycht vterance fors gan fycht reſt tary thay ſo contend sum confounding ſum defend ¶ eneas ſegit towne agane quene amata hyr ſelf wo ſlane tyme bargane enduring thus eneas moder fareſt dame venus mynd ſche put intent hald vnto wally incontinent ſtere oiſt ciete til aſſay wyth haiſly vnſet ſuddane effray grete myſcheif latynis tyl effere quhilk cumnyng tho vnwarnit mouing tyl eſpye turnus throw ſindry routis euery ſyde caſſin ee laſt behald cite saikles batal fre al ſic ſtryffe pane trauel quiet man wyffe ane greter bargane entent ſuddanly figure dyd emprent callis mneſtheus eik feregeſtus chif ani hys oiſt ſtrang sereſtus ane litill mote aſcendit hye quhare ſone forgadderit troyane army thyck hym flokkand baid bot nowthir ſcheild wapinnis doun thay laid amyd one knollis hicht vnto thaym ſpake thus herand euery wicht commandeneas cō mand men warre tary delay maid preceptis quhat ſal lay ſe man beſwere ſlaw rin tyl haiſty vnſet wyl begyn sen iupyter aſſiſtis ſyde herkis quhat purpois tyde thys day ſall deſtroy ſone bet doun laurent hale cyete toun quhilk caus al weryng quyte confounde king latinis • ing le wil thay relſaue bridil hand obeyſance grant comand ȝone hie turettis thay • p hie reikand chynais ȝounder ſe ſal mak plane equale ground quhat ſuld tary delay ane ſtound abiding ſic place quod quhyl turnus liſt fecht wyth v melle quhil ane vther time agane ouer cum vincuſt batal plane may haue refuge thys toun beleif syne efter feild v recounter gre •• cytezanis hede ciete welefare cheif iniquite twrs thidder hy hate byrnand fyre brandis aud wyth bleſand flammis ȝour handis renewis require agane ſaid trety ſworne promiſt ȝou quhen ſaid thay put thame array togiddir al ciete til aſſay thay pingil thraly quhay vnto portis firſt thaym met kelit entre doun bet sum vtheris ſchutis dartis takillis flanys thayin quhilk berinkin hede remanys wyth flicht ſchaftis thare thay dirknit ſkyis enee hym ſelf wyth formeſt thay brokin ſecund confederatioun ſworne mad amang cietezanis grete affray vprais diſtord monyſundry way sum bad vnclois ciete al faſt warp vp portis wide wallis caſt troyanis thare grete prince enee neuir ane dele mare langis cart fyft quheil thus ſen ȝe bene ane chriſten man large lay na ſic thing pray ȝou charge may ſuffyce vyrgyl ane end wait ſtory ierome ȝou kend quhow doung heft ſlepe gentilis bukis gaif ſyc kepe full ſcharp repreif ſum write ȝe wyſt ſentence haly pſalmiſt thay corruptit made abhominabyl thare ſtudying thing vnproffitabyl thus ſare dredis ſall thole ane hete graue ſtudy haue ſo lang forlete ȝa ſon quod wald thow eſchape ſa fayth ſall thus part ga think aſſonȝeis aſtart conſcience deuote hart fenȝe hym ierome counterfete quhare liggis bedouin lo ſwete lat wyt na heithin wycht gif thou afore tyme gane vnrycht followand ſa lang virgyll ane gentyle clerk quhy ſchrenkis thou ſchorte cryſtin werk thocht bot poetry ſay buke virgillis morale bene bot tway len ane fourtene nicht euir faderis ſaule gat quod thou ſall dere euir thou virgil knew wourd doun ſete drew syne club maid ane brade twenty rowtis apoun riging laid quhil deo meo merey cry richt hand ſtrekit vp hy hecht tranſlate tuke honour god appoſtlis twelf nowmer od glade thareof hand vp tuke syne went away fere wouke blent north eiſt wele fer saw gentyl iubar ſchynand day ſter chiron clepit ſigne ſagittary walkis ſomeris nycht bed cary ȝounder doun dwynis euin ſky away vpſpringis bricht dawning day till ane vthir place fer ſounder behald pleſance half wounder furth quencheing gan ſternes one one beſt bot lucifer allone forthirmore blaſin new day quhay micht diſiryue birdis bliſful bay beliue wyng beſſy lark vpſprang ſalute bricht morow hir ſang sone ouer feildis ſchynes licht clere welcum pilgryme baith lauborere tite hines gaif greif ane cry awalk fute go tyl huſbandry hird callis apoun page driue catall thare paſturage hynes wiffe clepis vp katherine gyl ȝa dame ſaid thay god wate ane gude wiſt dewye • rene powderit daſies gay schew ſward ane cullour dapil gray myſty vapouris ſpryngand vp ful ſwete maiſt confortabil glaid al mannis ſprete thareto thir birdis ſingis thare ſchawis menſtralis playis ioly day dawis thocht thus wil cunnand keip wil ane daw wyl ſleip complete promys ſchortly thus maid poete maiſter mapheus mak vp werk hereof clois buke may ſyne bot graue materis luke thocht ſtile virgil like full wele wate text ſal mony like syne eftir ane toung pen quhilk may ſuffice vulgar men quhay euer latine brute glore ſpeik na vers haue done lat clerkis ken poete different men vnletterit werk tak tent quhilk twiching xiii buke fere begynnis thus furth wyth followis finis ¶ xiii booke eneados ¶ rutulianis pepyl eftir turnus deceis obeyis eneas takis pece turnusmapheus reherſis quhat thī ge war done efter turnus ſlaughter latir bargane loiſt vincuſt feild ȝald furth fleand goiſt thys marciall prince rial lord enee victor ful mangnanymyte amyddis baith routis baldly ſtandis behald apoun athir handis aſtoniſt agaſt ware ſaw latine people hale raw ane felloun murnyng ane woful bere gan deuode hoiſtit ful clere depe thare breiſtis hard ſorow ſmert curage loiſt doun ſmytten thare hert like huge foreſt bewale granis doun bet branſchis ſkale quhen thay bene cached ſchakin faſt fell thud north wyndis blaſt thay thare lancis fixit erde lenys ſwerdis ane rerd thare ſcheildis thare ſchulderis ſtang away bargane faſt wary thay gan abhor hiars wylde lufe quhilk laitlye thay deſirit aprufe bridill refuſe thay dre ȝoik thare nekkis captiuite impiore gifnes greif quyet end harmys myſcheif quhen twa grete bullis plane togiddirrynnys byttir grete bargane thare lang debait mydland quhare thay ſtand large blude ſcheddand athir hand quhill athir thame vnto battellis ſyne awne beiſtis hirdis doi inclyne bot gif price victory betydis til ony thir twa athir ſidis anone catall quhilk fauourit langer beiſt ouercumin thare cheif thame ſubdewis vndir ward hye quhilk ouerhand wynnyng maſtery fre wil al thocht thare myndis thra aſſentis til obey euin richt ſa rutulianis al thocht grete ſite thare breiſtis bedowit ſmyte grete affray ſlauchter thare duke ȝit thocht thame leuir hale thare purpois tuke follow obey thare harmes gentill chiftane bettyr man armes thame ſubdew troiane enee beſeik pece amite reſt quyet euermore thame thare landis moblis vthir gere eneas tho wyth pleſand voce ful brade ſtand aboueexhortacion • ecircumſpects tymes cummyng mouing warre turnus thus ſayd dawnus ſon come haſty rage thy breiſt wyth foly dotage thou micht ſuffer troianis quhilkis commaund goddis thare planis power hie ioue ar hydder cary wythin boundis italite tary vane ſo excellyng wald thare beheſt promyſt hald lerne drede grete iouy ganeſtand fulfyl gladly goddis commaund thare greif wele aucht war sum tyme yre grow grete mupyter oft remembrance wykkit wrak soliſtis goddis tharof tak lo al ſic furour effere lattir meith terme preſent quhare aganis reſſoun equite aganis lawte brokin al vnite confederacioun ſworn band ar troiane pepyl ſare trublyt thou behold ſe extreme finale day gyf al vtheris gude exampil ay mot neuir leful agane tyll ony tyl contempne grete ioue vane rais wyth ſic drede effere sa vnwourthy mocioun wykkit beis glad bruke thine armour pled allace ane nobil corp lyggis dede grete turnus demnyng lauania coiſt na littyl thyng thou na ſchameeneas prudeut godly oracion nedis thynk na part eneas handis thou kelyt art cummys rutilyanis delay body ȝour duke turſis hyne away grant ȝou baith armour man hald tharto al ȝe langis vnto honour berying bewale deith ſic ane kyng bot grete paſſand gyrdyl ſic gere pallas dere freynd wount euander wyl ſend na lityl ſolace quhen ſal ſe felloun fa kelyt vnknaw ful glaid tharof turnus brocht daw netheles ȝe italyanis vthirwyſe bene clepit auſomanis remember hereof lerne tyme cummyng wyth better aſpectis happy begynning moue tak hand debait blyſſit ſternes brychteneas humanitye gentilnes ſwere neuer na oiſtis ȝit armour gla • dly aganis ȝou batal mouyt bot cunſtrenit ȝour furie kend wyth al force ſet defend troiane party awyne ſpryng al forſoith leifſum thyng eneas ſayd bot tharewyth addrſſeit towart ciete wall throw feyldis ſocht ful ioyuſlye new troiane reſſet herbry samin followis al rout attanis piſſance hale ȝoungkeris tewcranis ouer planis glaid wounder licht ſwift ſtedis foule flicht throw ſpede fute aſſayis oft bittir mouth cry fy accuſe latyne pepill oft faynt folkes ſleuthfull thaime call thare rerde bemyng quhare thay fare deray full hich dynnys ¶ eneas glaid victory louit goddis ſacrify thocht enee beſy thochtfull curis conſtrenit twiching ſepulturis folkis ſlane bering funerall fire flambis according ȝit neuertheles breiſt rollis ſteris ane grete mater largeare efferis bot firſt ſouerane honoure thare gyſe altaris detfull ſacrifice ordand fra hand hand efter rite vſance thare land ȝoung oxin gan thay ſteik ſla wythin thare tempil haue thay brocht alſua buſtuous ſwyne twinteris ſnaw quhite wyth clufis erde ſmyte wyth mony plat ſcheddand thare purpoure blude furth haue thay rent thare entraillys ful vnrude gan denude ſtriping thare hydis syne hakkyng thame tailȝeis ſydis hayt flambis brycht thame laid furth thay ȝet wyne coupis glaid god bachus gyftis faſt thay multiply wyth platis ful altaris gan charge wourſchip fat lyre ſmelland ſence vp bleſis fyre throw hald thay feiſt make gude chere vprais mery rerd ioyus bere thay extol louing wyth grete wounder grete iupiter fereful god thunder dame venus thay wourſchippit alſo saturnus dochter quene iuno pecifyit bettir ane huge laud thay ȝald tharfore eik ſelfe mar grete god armes thay magnify workar thare harmes syne hale remanent thare cumpany goddis thay name furth wyth hie vocis wyth loud cryis louit borne vp hie amang ſkyis thame al maiſt gratius eneas handis two cuſtum towart heum gan vplyft arrace ſyne chyld aſcaneus enbrace sayand ane wourdis al mycht thou ſon onlie chylde moiſt dere quham onlie reſtis thy faderis beleif quham throw ſa mony laubouris myſcheif caryit haueeneas cō forteth ſon efter gret laubouris cachit ful mony gatis hard fortoun thrawart fatis lo reſt quyet found ay lo reſt maiſt deſirit day mak end harmes diſtres paneful laubour paſſit expres lo acceptabil day euermore quhilk ful oft ſchawin quhen vntil hard bargane callit cum betid diſpoſicioun goddis abufe dereſt chyld thy behufe morne ſone aurora waxis rede ciete laurent rial ſtede ſal ſend victor ouir hand maiſter mantene land eftir turnyd agane vnto folkis pepyl troiane boddum breiſt wele law wyth ſoft ſpeche furth thir wourdis draw ȝe feris freyndis bald throw mony hard perrellis thik fald throw ſa feil ſtormis baith land ſe hidder caryit thys coiſt wyth throw ſa grete feruour batall ſtour doubil furie werefare armour ſa feil wynterys blaſtis tempeſtis al wayis noyfum vnreſtis horribil ȝit heuy woful hidduous wykkit vnhappy ȝit cruel myſcheuus ſtade bettir hope returne ȝour myndis beis glade end al ennoy wo terme cuming ſal thay ſtynt ho lyke deſyrit beſt wyth latyne pepill ferme peace reſt fal conione life vnite lauinia ilk blude quod quham defendit haue ſtrang bargane troiane kyn wyth blude italiane samyn mydlyt ſpous hy sal ȝeild lynnage reyng perpetually ane thing fallowis freyndis dere ȝou beſekyng ȝou requere bere ȝour myndis equale al anys commoun freyndis italianis fader law kyng latyne obeyis al wyth reuerence inclyne ane mychty ſcepture ryal weris mynd wyl perde bot batal douchty dedis armes ȝou wreik reuenge ȝour harmes lerne follow meik ȝe conterfete reuch piete eik quhat glore betid ful wele knaw bot heich heuin ſternes law wytneſſyng ſamyn wycht quhilk thou deliuerit fycht ſa huge harmes miſcheuys ſere ſal ȝou ſeis induce fer largeare rewardis mychtely ȝou rendir ȝour deſiret wyth ſic wourdis gan thame confortyng hys mynd ful mony ſundry thyng chancis bypaſt rollyng fro thinkand brocht reſt alſo na litil laubouris ſturt panis wyth excedand luf troianis ful ardently flowis al ioye glade laſt dangeare ennoy huge heuy perrellis mony fald thay war eſchapit brocht ſouir hald lyke quhen gredy glede hycht skummand vp turnus flycht wyth felloun fard watchand chykinnis lyte thare deith mannaſſand reddy ſmyt ereiſeit foule thare moder tho ful ſmart hir pullettis wyth harmes hir hart affray gretely wofull chance gan rax hir ſelf hir curage auance reſiſt hir fa ſcharpand hir bill hale force mycht egar apoun hir aduerſare baldlie fettis ſche quhill laſt gif bak fle mekill pane verray violence scho conſtranis pik hence hir birdis ſyne clokand ſcho ſekis raw affrayit doi thame ſamyn draw ennoyit greitlie hir childer dere quhen thay bene aſſemblit fere glaid ſcho wourdis thare mete ſcrap thay haif ſa grete perrell eſchaip nane vthir wiſe ſon anchiſes freyndlie wourdis thus amyd preis troyane myndis meſe aſſuage man fulfillit wit vaſſalage driuand furth thare hartis flocht hald drede birnand heuy thocht wele thame likis thare ioy eis laſt fundin eftir ſa grete diſeis lait fore tedious ſuffir ſuſtene ennoyus remember ſamin reherſing doi thame ſolace confort lykyng bot maiſt al grete enee quhilk excellent vertewe bounte excedit remanent ane fer way ſa ſeil dangeris mony affray goddis power mychty maieſte giftis grete offerandis wourſchippis eik iupiter fader goddis king gan extoll maiſt ſouerane louing ☞ turnus folkis made ſare regrete king latyne contempnis wrechit eſtate menetyme rutulianis yche one grete dede corp reuthfull wo begone thare duke turnus ſlane ſaid within ciete laurentum bare mekill murnyng thare myndis emprent thare ene ane large ſchoure furth ſent ofteris grete thocht heuin rane fer one brede dyd fyl eris twane kyng latyne cry womenting al irkyt nobill king breiſt ſelf tyme ballance rolling mony ſelcouth diuers chance bot quhen hard thare loude womenting increſſyng mare mare turnus ȝing wyth ſa griſly ane wound throw gird ſene mycht teris contene ſyne rout ſo triſt wo begone fail curtaſly chargis ſtyl anone baith wyth hys hand wourdis preſence intoned commanded ſilence lyke quhen fomy bere bet wyth hys thunderand awful tuſkis grete throw coiſt eik entrallys ane rout hound maiſt principall remanyng queſtyng ſort thys vnſilly chance offrayit ſchort wyth drawis maiſter hunter wyth quhyncheand mouthis quaik ſtandis fere grete ȝouling dyd complene mene bot thare lord raſis hys hand bedene byddis ceis thay hald thare mouthis ſtill thare quhyngeing thare queſting hys wyll refrenis clois gan thame withhald thir ſame wyſe thir rutulianis wald gan command debait thare voce ceice kingis mynd hald thare peace thus weping hart rute wele law king latyne begouth thir wourdis ſchaw grete motioun quhat altering vnſtabill oft ſyis interchangeitking latynis piteful oration deploring inconſtance toune reherſinge great • alamitys incommodytyis kingdomes commoun w • lthys variabill bene actis dedis men quod wyth grete trubil tranquilite quhirllit lyffe man behald dampnabill pride ambicioun wald bruke croun ſepture proude thine entent quhilk bene ſo fragil permanent fury luſt bene ouer gretumly bred ȝour breiſtis couate ſenȝeorie thou blynde deſire inſatiabil may tary mortal myndis quhiddir thou cary glory renowne lois vane conqueſt feil perrellis huge pane quhat condicioun quhat eſtate thou ſteris furth thir proude myndis infltate mony ſlichtis diſſatis quent thou turſis mony wayis ſchent feill tormentis grete harme wikkitnes quhat labour curis falſched craftynes mony dartis feyll ſwerdis kene gif thou beheld thou afore thy ene allace thou ſwete venom ſchawis ȝit warldly wourſchip dedelye bit allace ſorowful reward al thing realme thame couatis ryng quhilk coiſtis oft na litil thyng allace heuy birding warldly gere neuir houre may ſuffir promyt thare poſſeſſoure reſt pece ſit allace miſerabil chance hard eſtate kinglye honour ſa infortunate chance kingis ſtandis vnder lout mekil drede ay ſubiect dout thare eſtate decay ſuddanlie quiet eis tham deny turnus quhat aualit ſtere huge bargane ſo fere al italie ſic deray attanis perturbe ſtrang eneadanis conſtrenyng tham hard batall tyl aſſay quhat aualis pray ſay til haue brokin violate ſchent haly promyſſis bandis gent peace concord obliſt ſworne quhat thy mynd rent al torne ſa mekyl impacience wyſe thay liſt moue myne auiſe thy pepill ſo bald ſtrang ſage bene diſcendit goddis lynnage command ioue god thunder ar hiddir carryit mak ſic blunder wylfully motiue ſo beliue enforcit thame ouer coiſt dryue forth brek band promyſt douchter til gud ſon enee thy hand hard bargane ray ſtere quhen planely denyit moue ſa grete folie dotage inuoluit thy mynde furie rage oft quhen thou auful batall wend amyd routis thy ſtede aſſend ſchynand armour arrayit al rycht aſſayit wythdraw fycht feil tymes defendit forbad go way thou begunnyng al efferit quhen thou wald depart amyd ȝet ſtoppit wicht ſare hart bot al nathing mycht ſlyntin quhat haue ſufferit ſyne ſtandis wyth ciete wallis wytneſſing fute hate wyth tenementis bigginnis half doun bet aud large feildis ſtrowit quhite banis hale piſſance italyanis al waſtit diſtroyit thus alake huge ſlauchter miſcheuus wraik al feyldis waxin rede browne mennis quelling grete occiſioun lang abaſit ferful quaking drede hard laubour quhilk extreme nede age ſa oft vndertane ſa feil dangeris quhare remede nane bot turnus thou lyggis dede quhare nobil renoune thy ȝouth hede quhare thyne excellent hie curage quhydder went thy ſtrenth vaſſillage quhare ſtatly bewtie thy face quhare ſchinand fygure alace thy fare vyſage quhidder gone thy pleaſand forret ſchaiplie ene clere ha feil teris woful dolour ſmart sal thou turnus rendir dawnus hart large wepyng dule wa ouerfleyit ſal al ciete ardea bot thay ſal behald wyth ſiclake throw gyrd wyth ſchamful wound caucht bak na note na cowardice thy mynd thou degenerit kynd woful fader wil rede laſt ſal ſolace thy dede al thocht thy harmes doth ſore ſmert grete eneas ſwerd perſit thy hart ſayand thus teris piete chekis baith face ouer chargit syne turnand towart mekil rout reuthful corp ilk turnus ſtout bad turs away cary furth anone vntil faderis ciete wo begone commandit body cald al funeral pomp efter vſage ald ¶ turnus corp tyll ardea 〈◊〉 quhilk ſuddand fyre vrynt doun ſchent rutilianis anone al ane rout dede corp ſlane lay ſtert gentil body ſtout ȝoungkere thay haue addreſſit layd ane riche bere eik feil takynnis way reft troianis bargane bare thay baith helmis hors ſcheildis vthir gere swerdis githernis mony ſtalwart ſpere syne eftir wery cart furth went troiane ſlauchter hate blude al beſprent furth haldis wepand meteſtus cartare craft lere ledand ſtede bedouin al ſwete thekis wet flotterand teris grete quhilk ſtede caryit turnus oft tofore victore hame grete triumph glore ful pompuſite apoun ane vthir wyſe efter feruent ſlauchter inemyis ȝounder vtheris enuyroun beris thare armour ſcheildis turnit doun remanent ſyne hale barnage followis wepand knycht ſwane page haboundance mony trigland tere kyng latyne wyth al thame towart palace returne anone wyth mynd trublit triſt wo begone ſa excellent dede corp ſlane teris al ſamyn furth ȝettis euery ane bayth agit men matronus chylder lite ciete fillis wyth womenting ſite daunus fader wyſe wyttand ſo ſuld remane ſe ſic dule wo ſon ſtalwart ſprete ȝald maid end lattir bargane bald thus brocht toun dede feris wyth ſic plente bitter wepand teris ſamyn tyme vthir diſeis ſocht mekil ſaid dolour hauy thocht latyne pepill war ſet battall troyanis doun bet turnus het recent dede wyth hys blude littyt ground al rede ſuddane fyre within wallis hie vmbeſet halelye ardea ciete byggyngis hys fader wo begone brynt doun bet reky flambis ſchone returnis aſſis rede fyrie ſparkis eueyry ſted twynkland vpſpringis ſternes hye hope help may fundyn quhydder ſo vnto goddis lyking fatis liſt ſchaw ſum ſigne turnus deith horybyl battal ſlane quhen pepill ſaw remedy nane belife woful trublit citezanys thare drery breiſtis batand attanis gan faſt bewale pietuous wepand face vnhappy chance wrechyt cais lang rabill woman matron al thare fors fled reuchfully attanis bald flambis bry • bleſis ſtout like emotis blak rout ythandlie labouris beſy beildit vnder rute ane hye tre tyll ane clift thare bike duelling ſtede hyde thare lang ſum werk wyuter brede gif ſo betid thay fel ax ſmyte apoun treis ſchank theron byte crop weltis ground felloun ruſche griſly ſound thare ſmale cauernis brok rent ſpedely litill rout furth ſprentis wyll rede fleand thay wat quhare turſing thare bi • dingis affroi • lye thare like houſe ſyde ſnale schakand hyr toppit ſchell hir tale fleand birnand hett ſchodois fele ane lang tyme gan werſil wrele thriſtand faſt thare feit vnto wale ȝit hede force ſtrenthis frawart feruent flambis faſt drawis scho ſkaldis mony wrikis thrawis preiſſis eſchew ferefull hete nane vthir wiſe ſa feil perrellis grete thir wofull cietezanis gan thame ſelf ſlyng ruſchand trublit mynd tylane lyng bayth thare wiſt quhare away bot maiſt allace wellaway wyth reuthful vocis cryand heuin git kyng dawnus woful ſteuin tho amyd flambis furth wyth ardea foule quham heroun clepe betand hyr wyngis thay behald fle furth fyre heich vp bayth name takin ouer al quhare beris ciete ardea auld quhilom wyth wally towrys hye vntauld stude werelye wrocht ſtrenth grete defence chaunget ful quyte gone hence wyth wyngys wyde fleand bayth vp doun bot ane foule ane ryal toun aſtonyſt thys nyce new cace oft wounderus meruellis place quhilk ſemyt nothing lytyl thocht thay ſend war goddis hie pepil al coufuſyt ſtyl dyd ſtand thare burding thare ſchulderys cariand mouit nouther fute toung mouth kyng daunus thys affray vncouth ardent lufe ſmytyn deſire thys cheif cyite deſtroyt brynt fyre hard dolour ſorow ſmert haldys ful clois depe grauyng hys hart fra dawnus ſon turnus ſaw dede huge lamentatioun made ſtede amyd al thys deray grete effere fame dyſeis forryder
